    WHEN 0 THEN N'Pending'
    WHEN 1 THEN N'Approved'
    WHEN 2 THEN N'Rejected'
    WHEN 3 THEN N'CheckedOut'
    WHEN 4 THEN N'Returned'
    WHEN 5 THEN N'Cancelled'

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[BookId], [b0].[Title] AS [BookTitle], [b].[StartDate], [b].[EndDate], CASE [b].[Status]

    WHEN 1 THEN N'Approved'

    WHEN 3 THEN N'CheckedOut'

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[BookId], [b0].[Title] AS [BookTitle], [b].[StartDate], [b].[EndDate], CASE [b].[Status]
    WHEN 0 THEN N'Pending'
    WHEN 1 THEN N'Approved'

    WHEN 3 THEN N'CheckedOut'

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[BookId], [b0].[Title] AS [BookTitle], [b].[StartDate], [b].[EndDate], CASE [b].[Status]
    WHEN 0 THEN N'Pending'
    WHEN 1 THEN N'Approved'
    WHEN 2 THEN N'Rejected'
    WHEN 3 THEN N'CheckedOut'
    WHEN 4 THEN N'Returned'
    WHEN 5 THEN N'Cancelled'
    ELSE CAST([b].[Status] AS nvarchar(max))
END AS [Status]
FROM [BorrowRequests] AS [b]
